listeners. The band’s 2012 album, Shields, garnered critical acclaim from everyone from Pitchfork folks to Jay-Z and earned comparisons to the lush, catchy genius of Brian Wilson’s Pet Sounds. Grizzly Bear evolved quickly from one man’s adventures in Pro Tools into a full band that delivers a live show akin to a garden of psychedelic sonic delights.
